<a id="GovernorNoncesKeyed"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorNoncesKeyed` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorNoncesKeyed.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorNoncesKeyed.sol";
```

An extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) that extends existing nonce management to use [`NoncesKeyed`](utils#NoncesKeyed), where the key is the low-order 192 bits of the `proposalId`.
This is useful for voting by signature while maintaining separate sequences of nonces for each proposal.

<Callout>
Traditional (un-keyed) nonces are still supported and can continue to be used as if this extension was not present.
</Callout>

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorPreventLateQuorum` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorPreventLateQuorum.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorPreventLateQuorum.sol";
```

A module that ensures there is a minimum voting period after quorum is reached. This prevents a large voter from
swaying a vote and triggering quorum at the last minute, by ensuring there is always time for other voters to react
and try to oppose the decision.

If a vote causes quorum to be reached, the proposal's voting period may be extended so that it does not end before at
least a specified time has passed (the "vote extension" parameter). This parameter can be set through a governance
proposal.

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">
<h3 style={{ marginTop: "0"}}>Functions</h3>

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-constructor-uint48-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">constructor(uint48 initialVoteExtension)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-constructor-uint48-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Initializes the vote extension parameter: the time in either number of blocks or seconds (depending on the
governor clock mode) that is required to pass since the moment a proposal reaches quorum until its voting period
ends. If necessary the voting period will be extended beyond the one set during proposal creation.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-proposalDeadline-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">proposalDeadline(uint256 proposalId) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-proposalDeadline-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the proposal deadline, which may have been extended beyond that set at proposal creation, if the
proposal reached quorum late in the voting period. See [`Governor.proposalDeadline`](#Governor-proposalDeadline-uint256-).

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-_tallyUpdated-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_tallyUpdated(uint256 proposalId)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-_tallyUpdated-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Vote tally updated and detects if it caused quorum to be reached, potentially extending the voting period.

May emit a [`GovernorPreventLateQuorum.ProposalExtended`](#GovernorPreventLateQuorum-ProposalExtended-uint256-uint64-) event.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-lateQuorumVoteExtension--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">lateQuorumVoteExtension() → uint48</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-lateQuorumVoteExtension--">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the current value of the vote extension parameter: the number of blocks that are required to pass
from the time a proposal reaches quorum until its voting period ends.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-setLateQuorumVoteExtension-uint48-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">setLateQuorumVoteExtension(uint48 newVoteExtension)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-setLateQuorumVoteExtension-uint48-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Changes the [`GovernorPreventLateQuorum.lateQuorumVoteExtension`](#GovernorPreventLateQuorum-lateQuorumVoteExtension--). This operation can only be performed by the governance executor,
generally through a governance proposal.

Emits a [`GovernorPreventLateQuorum.LateQuorumVoteExtensionSet`](#GovernorPreventLateQuorum-LateQuorumVoteExtensionSet-uint64-uint64-) event.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-_setLateQuorumVoteExtension-uint48-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_setLateQuorumVoteExtension(uint48 newVoteExtension)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-_setLateQuorumVoteExtension-uint48-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Changes the [`GovernorPreventLateQuorum.lateQuorumVoteExtension`](#GovernorPreventLateQuorum-lateQuorumVoteExtension--). This is an internal function that can be exposed in a public function
like [`GovernorPreventLateQuorum.setLateQuorumVoteExtension`](#GovernorPreventLateQuorum-setLateQuorumVoteExtension-uint48-) if another access control mechanism is needed.

Emits a [`GovernorPreventLateQuorum.LateQuorumVoteExtensionSet`](#GovernorPreventLateQuorum-LateQuorumVoteExtensionSet-uint64-uint64-) event.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-ProposalExtended-uint256-uint64-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">ProposalExtended(uint256 indexed proposalId, uint64 extendedDeadline)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">event</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-ProposalExtended-uint256-uint64-">#</a>
</div>
</div>

<div className="px-4">

Emitted when a proposal deadline is pushed back due to reaching quorum late in its voting period.

</div>
</div>
<a id="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-LateQuorumVoteExtensionSet-uint64-uint64-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">LateQuorumVoteExtensionSet(uint64 oldVoteExtension, uint64 newVoteExtension)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">event</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorPreventLateQuorum-LateQuorumVoteExtensionSet-uint64-uint64-">#</a>
</div>
</div>

<div className="px-4">

Emitted when the [`GovernorPreventLateQuorum.lateQuorumVoteExtension`](#GovernorPreventLateQuorum-lateQuorumVoteExtension--) parameter is changed.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorProposalGuardian"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorProposalGuardian` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorProposalGuardian.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorProposalGuardian.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) which adds a proposal guardian that can cancel proposals at any stage in the proposal's lifecycle.

<Callout>
if the proposal guardian is not configured, then proposers take this role for their proposals.
</Callout>

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">

<a id="GovernorProposalGuardian-setProposalGuardian-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">setProposalGuardian(address newProposalGuardian)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">

</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Update the proposal guardian's address. This operation can only be performed through a governance proposal.

Emits a [`GovernorProposalGuardian.ProposalGuardianSet`](#GovernorProposalGuardian-ProposalGuardianSet-address-address-) event.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorProposalGuardian-_setProposalGuardian-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorProposalGuardian-_setProposalGuardian-address-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Internal setter for the proposal guardian.

Emits a [`GovernorProposalGuardian.ProposalGuardianSet`](#GovernorProposalGuardian-ProposalGuardianSet-address-address-) event.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorProposalGuardian-_validateCancel-uint256-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_validateCancel(uint256 proposalId, address caller) → bool</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorProposalGuardian-_validateCancel-uint256-address-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Override [`Governor._validateCancel`](#Governor-_validateCancel-uint256-address-) to implement the extended cancellation logic.

* The [`GovernorProposalGuardian.proposalGuardian`](#GovernorProposalGuardian-proposalGuardian--) can cancel any proposal at any point.
* If no proposal guardian is set, the [`IGovernor.proposalProposer`](#IGovernor-proposalProposer-uint256-) can cancel their proposals at any point.
* In any case, permissions defined in [`Governor._validateCancel`](#Governor-_validateCancel-uint256-address-) (or another override) remains valid.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorProposalGuardian-ProposalGuardianSet-address-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">ProposalGuardianSet(address oldProposalGuardian, address newProposalGuardian)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">event</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorProposalGuardian-ProposalGuardianSet-address-address-">#</a>
</div>
</div>

<div className="px-4">

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorSequentialProposalId"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorSequentialProposalId` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorSequentialProposalId.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorSequentialProposalId.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) that changes the numbering of proposal ids from the default hash-based approach to
sequential ids.

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">

<a id="GovernorSequentialProposalId-latestProposalId--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">

<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">latestProposalId() → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">

<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorSequentialProposalId-latestProposalId--">#</a>

Returns the latest proposal id. A return value of 0 means no proposals have been created yet.

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorSequentialProposalId-_propose-address---uint256---bytes---string-address-">#</a>
</div>

<div className="px-4">

See `IGovernor-_propose`.
Hook into the proposing mechanism to increment proposal count.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorSequentialProposalId-_initializeLatestProposalId-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_initializeLatestProposalId(uint256 newLatestProposalId)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorSequentialProposalId-_initializeLatestProposalId-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Internal function to set the [`GovernorSequentialProposalId.latestProposalId`](#GovernorSequentialProposalId-latestProposalId--). This function is helpful when transitioning
from another governance system. The next proposal id will be `newLatestProposalId` + 1.

May only call this function if the current value of [`GovernorSequentialProposalId.latestProposalId`](#GovernorSequentialProposalId-latestProposalId--) is 0.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorSequentialProposalId-GovernorAlreadyInitializedLatestProposalId--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">GovernorAlreadyInitializedLatestProposalId()</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">error</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorSequentialProposalId-GovernorAlreadyInitializedLatestProposalId--">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

The [`GovernorSequentialProposalId.latestProposalId`](#GovernorSequentialProposalId-latestProposalId--) may only be initialized if it hasn't been set yet
(through initialization or the creation of a proposal).

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorStorage"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorStorage` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorStorage.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorStorage.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) that implements storage of proposal details. This module also provides primitives for
the enumerability of proposals.

Use cases for this module include:
- UIs that explore the proposal state without relying on event indexing.
- Using only the proposalId as an argument in the [`Governor.queue`](#Governor-queue-address---uint256---bytes---bytes32-) and [`Governor.execute`](#Governor-execute-address---uint256---bytes---bytes32-) functions for L2 chains
  where storage is cheap compared to calldata.

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">
<h3 style={{ marginTop: "0"}}>Functions</h3>

<a id="GovernorSuperQuorum"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorSuperQuorum` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorSuperQuorum.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorSuperQuorum.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) with a super quorum. Proposals that meet the super quorum (and have a majority of for
votes) advance to the `Succeeded` state before the proposal deadline. Counting modules that want to use this
extension must implement [`GovernorCountingFractional.proposalVotes`](#GovernorCountingFractional-proposalVotes-uint256-).

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">

<a id="GovernorSuperQuorum-superQuorum-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">superQuorum(uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorSuperQuorum-superQuorum-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Minimum number of cast votes required for a proposal to reach super quorum. Only FOR votes are counted
towards the super quorum. Once the super quorum is reached, an active proposal can proceed to the next state
without waiting for the proposal deadline.

<Callout>
The `timepoint` parameter corresponds to the snapshot used for counting the vote. This enables scaling of the
quorum depending on values such as the `totalSupply` of a token at this timepoint (see [`ERC20Votes`](token/ERC20#ERC20Votes)).
</Callout>

<Callout>
Make sure the value specified for the super quorum is greater than [`Governor.quorum`](#Governor-quorum-uint256-), otherwise, it may be
possible to pass a proposal with less votes than the default quorum.
</Callout>

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorSuperQuorum-proposalVotes-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">proposalVotes(uint256 proposalId) → uint256 againstVotes, uint256 forVotes, uint256 abstainVotes</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorSuperQuorum-proposalVotes-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Accessor to the internal vote counts. This must be implemented by the counting module. Counting modules
that don't implement this function are incompatible with this module

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorSuperQuorum-state-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">state(uint256 proposalId) → enum IGovernor.ProposalState</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorSuperQuorum-state-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Overridden version of the [`Governor.state`](#Governor-state-uint256-) function that checks if the proposal has reached the super
quorum.

<Callout>
If the proposal reaches super quorum but [`Governor._voteSucceeded`](#Governor-_voteSucceeded-uint256-) returns false, eg, assuming the super quorum
has been set low enough that both FOR and AGAINST votes have exceeded it and AGAINST votes exceed FOR votes,
the proposal continues to be active until [`Governor._voteSucceeded`](#Governor-_voteSucceeded-uint256-) returns true or the proposal deadline is reached.
This means that with a low super quorum it is also possible that a vote can succeed prematurely before enough
AGAINST voters have a chance to vote. Hence, it is recommended to set a high enough super quorum to avoid these
types of scenarios.
</Callout>

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorTimelockAccess"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorTimelockAccess` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorTimelockAccess.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorTimelockAccess.sol";
```

This module connects a [`Governor`](#Governor) instance to an [`AccessManager`](access#AccessManager) instance, allowing the governor to make calls
that are delay-restricted by the manager using the normal [`Governor.queue`](#Governor-queue-address---uint256---bytes---bytes32-) workflow. An optional base delay is applied to
operations that are not delayed externally by the manager. Execution of a proposal will be delayed as much as
necessary to meet the required delays of all of its operations.

This extension allows the governor to hold and use its own assets and permissions, unlike [`GovernorTimelockControl`](#GovernorTimelockControl)
and [`GovernorTimelockCompound`](#GovernorTimelockCompound), where the timelock is a separate contract that must be the one to hold assets and
permissions. Operations that are delay-restricted by the manager, however, will be executed through the
[`AccessManager.execute`](access#AccessManager-execute-address-bytes-) function.

==== Security Considerations

Some operations may be cancelable in the `AccessManager` by the admin or a set of guardians, depending on the
restricted function being invoked. Since proposals are atomic, the cancellation by a guardian of a single operation
in a proposal will cause all of the proposal to become unable to execute. Consider proposing cancellable operations
separately.

By default, function calls will be routed through the associated `AccessManager` whenever it claims the target
function to be restricted by it. However, admins may configure the manager to make that claim for functions that a
governor would want to call directly (e.g., token transfers) in an attempt to deny it access to those functions. To
mitigate this attack vector, the governor is able to ignore the restrictions claimed by the `AccessManager` using
[`GovernorTimelockAccess.setAccessManagerIgnored`](#GovernorTimelockAccess-setAccessManagerIgnored-address-bytes4---bool-). While permanent denial of service is mitigated, temporary DoS may still be technically
possible. All of the governor's own functions (e.g., [`GovernorTimelockAccess.setBaseDelaySeconds`](#GovernorTimelockAccess-setBaseDelaySeconds-uint32-)) ignore the `AccessManager` by default.

<Callout>
`AccessManager` does not support scheduling more than one operation with the same target and calldata at
the same time. See [`AccessManager.schedule`](access#AccessManager-schedule-address-bytes-uint48-) for a workaround.
</Callout>

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">

<a id="GovernorTimelockAccess-accessManager--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorTimelockAccess-accessManager--">#</a>

<a id="GovernorTimelockAccess-baseDelaySeconds--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">baseDelaySeconds() → uint32</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorTimelockAccess-baseDelaySeconds--">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Base delay that will be applied to all function calls. Some may be further delayed by their associated
`AccessManager` authority; in this case the final delay will be the maximum of the base delay and the one
demanded by the authority.

<Callout>
Execution delays are processed by the `AccessManager` contracts, and according to that contract are
expressed in seconds. Therefore, the base delay is also in seconds, regardless of the governor's clock mode.
</Callout>

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorTimelockAccess-setBaseDelaySeconds-uint32-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">

<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorTimelockAccess-setBaseDelaySeconds-uint32-">#</a>
</div>

those that must be scheduled are cancellable by `AccessManager` guardians.

Mechanism to queue a proposal, potentially scheduling some of its operations in the AccessManager.

<Callout>
The execution delay is chosen based on the delay information retrieved in [`Governor.propose`](#Governor-propose-address---uint256---bytes---string-). This value may be
off if the delay was updated since proposal creation. In this case, the proposal needs to be recreated.
</Callout>

<a id="GovernorTimelockCompound"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorTimelockCompound` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorTimelockCompound.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorTimelockCompound.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) that binds the execution process to a Compound Timelock. This adds a delay, enforced by
the external timelock to all successful proposals (in addition to the voting duration). The [`Governor`](#Governor) needs to be
the admin of the timelock for any operation to be performed. A public, unrestricted,
[`GovernorTimelockCompound.__acceptAdmin`](#GovernorTimelockCompound-__acceptAdmin--) is available to accept ownership of the timelock.

Using this model means the proposal will be operated by the [`TimelockController`](#TimelockController) and not by the [`Governor`](#Governor). Thus,
the assets and permissions must be attached to the [`TimelockController`](#TimelockController). Any asset sent to the [`Governor`](#Governor) will be
inaccessible from a proposal, unless executed via [`Governor.relay`](#Governor-relay-address-uint256-bytes-).

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">
<h3 style={{ marginTop: "0"}}>Functions</h3>
<div className="font-mono">
- [constructor(timelockAddress)](#GovernorTimelockCompound-constructor-contract-ICompoundTimelock-)

<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">__acceptAdmin()</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorTimelockCompound-__acceptAdmin--">#</a>

<a id="GovernorTimelockCompound-updateTimelock-contract-ICompoundTimelock-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">updateTimelock(contract ICompoundTimelock newTimelock)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorTimelockCompound-updateTimelock-contract-ICompoundTimelock-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Public endpoint to update the underlying timelock instance. Restricted to the timelock itself, so updates
must be proposed, scheduled, and executed through governance proposals.

For security reasons, the timelock must be handed over to another admin before setting up a new one. The two
operations (hand over the timelock) and do the update can be batched in a single proposal.

Note that if the timelock admin has been handed over in a previous operation, we refuse updates made through the
timelock if admin of the timelock has already been accepted and the operation is executed outside the scope of
governance.

CAUTION: It is not recommended to change the timelock while there are other queued governance proposals.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorTimelockCompound-TimelockChange-address-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">event</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorTimelockCompound-TimelockChange-address-address-">#</a>
</div>
</div>

<div className="px-4">

Emitted when the timelock controller used for proposal execution is modified.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorTimelockControl"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorTimelockControl` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorTimelockControl.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorTimelockControl.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) that binds the execution process to an instance of [`TimelockController`](#TimelockController). This adds a
delay, enforced by the [`TimelockController`](#TimelockController) to all successful proposals (in addition to the voting duration). The
[`Governor`](#Governor) needs the proposer (and ideally the executor and canceller) roles for the [`Governor`](#Governor) to work properly.

Using this model means the proposal will be operated by the [`TimelockController`](#TimelockController) and not by the [`Governor`](#Governor). Thus,
the assets and permissions must be attached to the [`TimelockController`](#TimelockController). Any asset sent to the [`Governor`](#Governor) will be
inaccessible from a proposal, unless executed via [`Governor.relay`](#Governor-relay-address-uint256-bytes-).

<Callout type="warn">
Setting up the TimelockController to have additional proposers or cancelers besides the governor is very
risky, as it grants them the ability to: 1) execute operations as the timelock, and thus possibly performing
operations or accessing funds that are expected to only be accessible through a vote, and 2) block governance
proposals that have been approved by the voters, effectively executing a Denial of Service attack.
</Callout>

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">

</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Public endpoint to update the underlying timelock instance. Restricted to the timelock itself, so updates
must be proposed, scheduled, and executed through governance proposals.

CAUTION: It is not recommended to change the timelock while there are other queued governance proposals.

</div>

## `GovernorVotes` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorVotes.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorVotes.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) for voting weight extraction from an [`ERC20Votes`](token/ERC20#ERC20Votes) token, or since v4.5 an [`ERC721Votes`](token/ERC721#ERC721Votes)
token.

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorVotesQuorumFraction` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorVotesQuorumFraction.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorVotesQuorumFraction.sol";
```

Extension of [`Governor`](#Governor) for voting weight extraction from an [`ERC20Votes`](token/ERC20#ERC20Votes) token and a quorum expressed as a
fraction of the total supply.

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">
<h3 style={{ marginTop: "0"}}>Functions</h3>
<div className="font-mono">
- [constructor(quorumNumeratorValue)](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-constructor-uint256-)
- [quorumNumerator()](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumNumerator--)
- [quorumNumerator(timepoint)](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumNumerator-uint256-)
- [quorumDenominator()](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumDenominator--)

<a id="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-constructor-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">constructor(uint256 quorumNumeratorValue)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-constructor-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Initialize quorum as a fraction of the token's total supply.

The fraction is specified as `numerator / denominator`. By default the denominator is 100, so quorum is
specified as a percent: a numerator of 10 corresponds to quorum being 10% of total supply. The denominator can be
customized by overriding [`GovernorVotesQuorumFraction.quorumDenominator`](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumDenominator--).

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumNumerator--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">quorumNumerator() → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumNumerator--">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the current quorum numerator. See [`GovernorVotesQuorumFraction.quorumDenominator`](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumDenominator--).

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumNumerator-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">quorumNumerator(uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumNumerator-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the quorum numerator at a specific timepoint. See [`GovernorVotesQuorumFraction.quorumDenominator`](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumDenominator--).

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumDenominator--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">quorumDenominator() → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorumDenominator--">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the quorum denominator. Defaults to 100, but may be overridden.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorum-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">quorum(uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-quorum-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the quorum for a timepoint, in terms of number of votes: `supply * numerator / denominator`.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-updateQuorumNumerator-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">updateQuorumNumerator(uint256 newQuorumNumerator)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-updateQuorumNumerator-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Changes the quorum numerator.

Emits a [`GovernorVotesQuorumFraction.QuorumNumeratorUpdated`](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-QuorumNumeratorUpdated-uint256-uint256-) event.

Requirements:

- Must be called through a governance proposal.
- New numerator must be smaller or equal to the denominator.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-_updateQuorumNumerator-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-_updateQuorumNumerator-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Changes the quorum numerator.

Emits a [`GovernorVotesQuorumFraction.QuorumNumeratorUpdated`](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-QuorumNumeratorUpdated-uint256-uint256-) event.

Requirements:

- New numerator must be smaller or equal to the denominator.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/extensions/GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction.sol";
```

Extension of [`GovernorVotesQuorumFraction`](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction) with a super quorum expressed as a
fraction of the total supply. Proposals that meet the super quorum (and have a majority of for votes) advance to
the `Succeeded` state before the proposal deadline.

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">
<h3 style={{ marginTop: "0"}}>Functions</h3>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-constructor-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">constructor(uint256 superQuorumNumeratorValue)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-constructor-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Initialize super quorum as a fraction of the token's total supply.

The super quorum is specified as a fraction of the token's total supply and has to
be greater than the quorum.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-superQuorumNumerator--"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">superQuorumNumerator() → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-superQuorumNumerator--">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the current super quorum numerator.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-superQuorumNumerator-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">superQuorumNumerator(uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-superQuorumNumerator-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the super quorum numerator at a specific `timepoint`.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-superQuorum-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">superQuorum(uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-superQuorum-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the super quorum for a `timepoint`, in terms of number of votes: `supply * numerator / denominator`.
See [`GovernorSuperQuorum.superQuorum`](#GovernorSuperQuorum-superQuorum-uint256-) for more details.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-updateSuperQuorumNumerator-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">updateSuperQuorumNumerator(uint256 newSuperQuorumNumerator)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-updateSuperQuorumNumerator-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Changes the super quorum numerator.

Emits a [`GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction.SuperQuorumNumeratorUpdated`](#GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-SuperQuorumNumeratorUpdated-uint256-uint256-) event.

Requirements:

- Must be called through a governance proposal.
- New super quorum numerator must be smaller or equal to the denominator.
- New super quorum numerator must be greater than or equal to the quorum numerator.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-_updateSuperQuorumNumerator-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_updateSuperQuorumNumerator(uint256 newSuperQuorumNumerator)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-_updateSuperQuorumNumerator-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Changes the super quorum numerator.

Emits a [`GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction.SuperQuorumNumeratorUpdated`](#GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-SuperQuorumNumeratorUpdated-uint256-uint256-) event.

Requirements:

- New super quorum numerator must be smaller or equal to the denominator.
- New super quorum numerator must be greater than or equal to the quorum numerator.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-_updateQuorumNumerator-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_updateQuorumNumerator(uint256 newQuorumNumerator)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-_updateQuorumNumerator-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Overrides [`GovernorVotesQuorumFraction._updateQuorumNumerator`](#GovernorVotesQuorumFraction-_updateQuorumNumerator-uint256-) to ensure the super
quorum numerator is greater than or equal to the quorum numerator.

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-state-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">state(uint256 proposalId) → enum IGovernor.ProposalState</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-state-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Overridden version of the [`Governor.state`](#Governor-state-uint256-) function that checks if the proposal has reached the super
quorum.

<Callout>
If the proposal reaches super quorum but [`Governor._voteSucceeded`](#Governor-_voteSucceeded-uint256-) returns false, eg, assuming the super quorum
has been set low enough that both FOR and AGAINST votes have exceeded it and AGAINST votes exceed FOR votes,
the proposal continues to be active until [`Governor._voteSucceeded`](#Governor-_voteSucceeded-uint256-) returns true or the proposal deadline is reached.
This means that with a low super quorum it is also possible that a vote can succeed prematurely before enough
AGAINST voters have a chance to vote. Hence, it is recommended to set a high enough super quorum to avoid these
types of scenarios.
</Callout>

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-SuperQuorumNumeratorUpdated-uint256-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">SuperQuorumNumeratorUpdated(uint256 oldSuperQuorumNumerator, uint256 newSuperQuorumNumerator)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">event</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-SuperQuorumNumeratorUpdated-uint256-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>

<div className="px-4">

</div>
</div>

<a id="GovernorVotesSuperQuorumFraction-GovernorInvalidSuperQuorumFraction-uint256-uint256-"></a>

## `IVotes` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/utils/IVotes.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/utils/IVotes.sol";
```

Common interface for [`ERC20Votes`](token/ERC20#ERC20Votes), [`ERC721Votes`](token/ERC721#ERC721Votes), and other [`Votes`](#Votes)-enabled contracts.

<div className="bg-secondary p-4 rounded-md mb-6">
<h3 style={{ marginTop: "0"}}>Functions</h3>
<div className="font-mono">
- [getVotes(account)](#IVotes-getVotes-address-)
- [getPastVotes(account, timepoint)](#IVotes-getPastVotes-address-uint256-)
- [getPastTotalSupply(timepoint)](#IVotes-getPastTotalSupply-uint256-)

- [delegate(delegatee)](#IVotes-delegate-address-)
- [delegateBySig(delegatee, nonce, expiry, v, r, s)](#IVotes-delegateBySig-address-uint256-uint256-uint8-bytes32-bytes32-)
</div>
</div>

<a id="IVotes-getVotes-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">getVotes(address account) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">

Returns the current amount of votes that `account` has.

</div>
</div>

<a id="IVotes-getPastVotes-address-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">getPastVotes(address account, uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">external</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="IVotes-getPastVotes-address-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the amount of votes that `account` had at a specific moment in the past. If the `clock()` is
configured to use block numbers, this will return the value at the end of the corresponding block.

</div>
</div>

<a id="IVotes-getPastTotalSupply-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">getPastTotalSupply(uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">external</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="IVotes-getPastTotalSupply-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the total supply of votes available at a specific moment in the past. If the `clock()` is
configured to use block numbers, this will return the value at the end of the corresponding block.

<Callout>
This value is the sum of all available votes, which is not necessarily the sum of all delegated votes.
Votes that have not been delegated are still part of total supply, even though they would not participate in a
vote.
</Callout>

</div>
</div>

<a id="IVotes-delegates-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">external</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="IVotes-delegates-address-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the delegate that `account` has chosen.

</div>
</div>

## `Votes` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/utils/Votes.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/utils/Votes.sol";
```

This is a base abstract contract that tracks voting units, which are a measure of voting power that can be
transferred, and provides a system of vote delegation, where an account can delegate its voting units to a sort of
"representative" that will pool delegated voting units from different accounts and can then use it to vote in
decisions. In fact, voting units _must_ be delegated in order to count as actual votes, and an account has to
delegate those votes to itself if it wishes to participate in decisions and does not have a trusted representative.

This contract is often combined with a token contract such that voting units correspond to token units. For an
example, see [`ERC721Votes`](token/ERC721#ERC721Votes).

The full history of delegate votes is tracked on-chain so that governance protocols can consider votes as distributed
at a particular block number to protect against flash loans and double voting. The opt-in delegate system makes the
cost of this history tracking optional.

When using this module the derived contract must implement [`Votes._getVotingUnits`](#Votes-_getVotingUnits-address-) (for example, make it return
[`ERC721.balanceOf`](token/ERC721#ERC721-balanceOf-address-)), and can use [`Votes._transferVotingUnits`](#Votes-_transferVotingUnits-address-address-uint256-) to track a change in the distribution of those units (in the
previous example, it would be included in [`ERC721._update`](token/ERC721#ERC721-_update-address-uint256-address-)).

<div className="px-4">

Clock used for flagging checkpoints. Can be overridden to implement timestamp based
checkpoints (and voting), in which case [`Governor.CLOCK_MODE`](#Governor-CLOCK_MODE--) should be overridden as well to match.

</div>

<a id="Votes-getPastVotes-address-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">getPastVotes(address account, uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="Votes-getPastVotes-address-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the amount of votes that `account` had at a specific moment in the past. If the `clock()` is
configured to use block numbers, this will return the value at the end of the corresponding block.

Requirements:

- `timepoint` must be in the past. If operating using block numbers, the block must be already mined.

</div>
</div>

<a id="Votes-getPastTotalSupply-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">getPastTotalSupply(uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="Votes-getPastTotalSupply-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the total supply of votes available at a specific moment in the past. If the `clock()` is
configured to use block numbers, this will return the value at the end of the corresponding block.

<Callout>
This value is the sum of all available votes, which is not necessarily the sum of all delegated votes.
Votes that have not been delegated are still part of total supply, even though they would not participate in a
vote.
</Callout>

Requirements:

- `timepoint` must be in the past. If operating using block numbers, the block must be already mined.

</div>
</div>

<a id="VotesExtended"></a>

<div style={{marginTop: "4em"}} className="w-full flex flex-row items-center justify-between">

## `VotesExtended` 

<a target="_blank" style={{marginTop: "1.5em"}} href="https://github.com/OpenZeppelin/openzeppelin-contracts/blob/v5.4.0/contracts/governance/utils/VotesExtended.sol">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-github-icon lucide-github"><path d="M15 22v-4a4.8 4.8 0 0 0-1-3.5c3 0 6-2 6-5.5.08-1.25-.27-2.48-1-3.5.28-1.15.28-2.35 0-3.5 0 0-1 0-3 1.5-2.64-.5-5.36-.5-8 0C6 2 5 2 5 2c-.3 1.15-.3 2.35 0 3.5A5.403 5.403 0 0 0 4 9c0 3.5 3 5.5 6 5.5-.39.49-.68 1.05-.85 1.65-.17.6-.22 1.23-.15 1.85v4"/><path d="M9 18c-4.51 2-5-2-7-2"/></svg>
</a>

</div>

```solidity
import "@openzeppelin/contracts/governance/utils/VotesExtended.sol";
```

Extension of [`Votes`](#Votes) that adds checkpoints for delegations and balances.

<Callout type="warn">
While this contract extends [`Votes`](#Votes), valid uses of [`Votes`](#Votes) may not be compatible with
[`VotesExtended`](#VotesExtended) without additional considerations. This implementation of [`Votes._transferVotingUnits`](#Votes-_transferVotingUnits-address-address-uint256-) must
run AFTER the voting weight movement is registered, such that it is reflected on [`Votes._getVotingUnits`](#Votes-_getVotingUnits-address-).
</Callout>

Said differently, [`VotesExtended`](#VotesExtended) MUST be integrated in a way that calls [`Votes._transferVotingUnits`](#Votes-_transferVotingUnits-address-address-uint256-) AFTER the
asset transfer is registered and balances are updated:

```solidity
contract VotingToken is Token, VotesExtended {
  function transfer(address from, address to, uint256 tokenId) public override {
    super.transfer(from, to, tokenId); // <- Perform the transfer first ...
    _transferVotingUnits(from, to, 1); // <- ... then call _transferVotingUnits.
  }

  function _getVotingUnits(address account) internal view override returns (uint256) {
     return balanceOf(account);
  }
}
```

[`ERC20Votes`](token/ERC20#ERC20Votes) and [`ERC721Votes`](token/ERC721#ERC721Votes) follow this pattern and are thus safe to use with [`VotesExtended`](#VotesExtended).

<a id="VotesExtended-getPastDelegate-address-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">getPastDelegate(address account, uint256 timepoint) → address</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="VotesExtended-getPastDelegate-address-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the delegate of an `account` at a specific moment in the past. If the `clock()` is
configured to use block numbers, this will return the value at the end of the corresponding block.

Requirements:

- `timepoint` must be in the past. If operating using block numbers, the block must be already mined.

</div>
</div>

<a id="VotesExtended-getPastBalanceOf-address-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">getPastBalanceOf(address account, uint256 timepoint) → uint256</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">public</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="VotesExtended-getPastBalanceOf-address-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Returns the `balanceOf` of an `account` at a specific moment in the past. If the `clock()` is
configured to use block numbers, this will return the value at the end of the corresponding block.

Requirements:

- `timepoint` must be in the past. If operating using block numbers, the block must be already mined.

</div>
</div>

<a id="VotesExtended-_delegate-address-address-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_delegate(address account, address delegatee)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="VotesExtended-_delegate-address-address-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Delegate all of `account`'s voting units to `delegatee`.

Emits events [`IVotes.DelegateChanged`](#IVotes-DelegateChanged-address-address-address-) and [`IVotes.DelegateVotesChanged`](#IVotes-DelegateVotesChanged-address-uint256-uint256-).

</div>
</div>

<a id="VotesExtended-_transferVotingUnits-address-address-uint256-"></a>

<div className="border rounded-md mb-4">
<div className="bg-secondary flex w-full justify-between px-4">
<p className="font-bold text-sm font-mono">_transferVotingUnits(address from, address to, uint256 amount)</p>
<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-2">
<p className="font-light text-sm">internal</p>
<a className="peer" data-card href="VotesExtended-_transferVotingUnits-address-address-uint256-">#</a>
</div>
</div>
<div className="px-4">

Transfers, mints, or burns voting units. To register a mint, `from` should be zero. To register a burn, `to`
should be zero. Total supply of voting units will be adjusted with mints and burns.

</div>
</div>
